window.onerror = function onErrorFunc(msg, url, line, colno, error) {
if(!window.ta || !ta.has('ta.js_error_array.processed')) {
if(typeof js_error_array == 'undefined') {
js_error_array = [];
}
var err = error;
js_error_array[js_error_array.length] = {'msg': msg, 'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'error': err, 'ready_state': document.readyState};
return true;
}
else {
if(window.ta && ta.util && ta.util.error && ta.util.error.record) {
ta.util.error.record(error, 'error post load:: ' + msg, null, {'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'ready_state': document.readyState});
}
}
};
</script>

           <div class="modules-membercenter-about-me " data-ox-name="modules.membercenter.AboutMe" data-ox-context="MemberCenter_ProfileData, Errors, Member"> 
            <div class="aboutMe profileBox">
             <span class="header">About Me</span> 
             <div class="info">
              <p>Since May 2004</p>
              <p>Lives in Boston, MA</p>
              <p> 35-49 year old female </p>
              <p>I'm a mother of four and a budget traveler. I do splurge occasionally when I go away with my husband or other adults but I always try to get the best value for my money. I love to travel but being a Mom keeps me closer to home. If I can't go far, I try to take advantage of all the wonderful day trips I can visit locally. I frequently take my children to the local museums, walks, historical sites, and/or special events whenever we can. We are members of a local children's museum and zoo members. We use our membership for free visits to reciprocal museums and zoos. I also take advantage of free admission days at the other local museums and take advantage of library passes. I occasionally use the discounts coupons offered from the 'Entertainment Book' or from 'Restaurant.Com' To be able to take advantage of all the great restaurants in the area, I try to dine at lunch time to save a few dollars or order from the bar menu. Every year, as a family, we go on a least 6 local overnight trips. My husband and I try to squeeze a few weekends away without the children and occasionally I will travel with my extended family or go solo. I love Hotwire.com and have stayed at some wonderful 4 star hotels for a fraction of the rack rates. For the past few years, as a family we have started to do repeat trips to Newport, RI for New Year's and February School Vacation week and Hyannis, Cape Cod for April School Vacation week and a week in August, for these trips we stay at budget, family friendly motels. We also spend many of our vacation days in Meredith, NH in our extended family's vacation home. I try to do an international trip once every two or three years, most of the time it's to Germany where I have extended family. </p>
             </div>
            </div> 
           </div>
